   <script type="text/javascript">
    $('.et_cc_wz_track').click(function(){
     if(et_cc_wz_pagename && et_cc_wz_area) {
       et_eC_Wrapper('y5EDSE','' + et_cc_wz_pagename, et_cc_wz_area);
       et_cc_wrapper('O74s6QuK7zIrJgBcSEB4se+sfIUGtSWS8xCIa9AmJVg=',{cc_pagename:'' + et_cc_wz_pagename})
     }

   <script type="text/javascript">
    if(typeof et_cc_mode != 'undefined') {
     if(typeof etr_adding != 'undefined' && etr_adding == ''){
       etr_adding = '--'
     }
     sendCampaignControlEvent(et_cc_mode)
   }
 
   function sendCampaignControlEvent(aETCCMode) {
     
     if(typeof etr_variants == 'undefined') {
       etr_variants = '';
     }
     
     if(typeof etr_duration == 'undefined') {
       etr_duration = '--';
     }
     
     if(typeof etCommerce == 'undefined') {
       return;
     }
   
     if(aETCCMode == "prereceipt") {
       
       if(typeof et_basket_id == 'undefined') {
         return;
       }
   
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Insert To Basket auf Vorquittung */
       
       var product =
       {
         id      :etr_id,
         name    :etr_name,
         category:[etr_game,etr_gamename,etr_day],
         price   :etr_price,
         currency:'EUR',
         variants:
         {
           'Zusatzspiel' : checkVariants(etr_adding),
           'Laufzeit' : checkVariants(etr_duration),
           'Spezial' : checkVariants(etr_variants)
         }
       };
       etCommerce.sendEvent('insertToBasket', product, 1, et_basket_id);
       
       $('.et_cc_removeFromBasket').click(function(){
         /* Campaign Control Tracking: Remove From Basket auf Vorquittung */
         etCommerce.sendEvent('removeFromBasket', product, 1, et_basket_id);
       });
     
     } else if (aETCCMode == "receipt") {
       
       if(typeof et_basket_id == 'undefined') {
         return;
       }
     
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Order auf Quittung */
       
       var basket =
       {
         id: et_basket_id,
         products:[
         {
           product:
           {
             id      :etr_id,
             name    :etr_name,
             category:[etr_game,etr_gamename,etr_day],
             price   :etr_price,
             currency:'EUR',
             variants:
             {
               'Zusatzspiel' : checkVariants(etr_adding),
               'Laufzeit' : checkVariants(etr_duration),
               'Spezial' : checkVariants(etr_variants)
             }
           },
           quantity:1
         }]
       }
       
       var order =
       {
         orderNumber:getGlobalIdentifier(),
         status:'sale',
         orderPrice:etr_price,
         currency:'EUR',
         basket:basket,
         customerGroup:'Stammkunde',
         paymentMethod:etr_payment
       }
       etCommerce.sendEvent('order',order,'Warenkorb');
     
     } else if(aETCCMode == "register") {
       var guid = getGlobalIdentifier();
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Order auf Registrierung */
       console.log("register tracking");
       
       var basket =
       {
         id:guid,
         products:[
         {
           product:
           {
             id      :'REG',
             name    :'Registrierung',
             category:['Registrierung'],
             price   :'1.00',
             currency:'EUR',
             variants:{'Reg':'Reg'}
           },
           quantity:1
         }]
       };
   
       var order =
       {
         orderNumber:Date.now().toString(),
         status:'lead',
         orderPrice:'1.00',
         currency:'EUR',
         basket:basket,
         customerGroup:'18'
       };
       etCommerce.sendEvent('order',order,'Registrierung');
       
     }
   }
   
   /* Helper functions */
   
   function getGlobalIdentifier() {
     function s4() {
       return Math.floor((1 + Math.random()) * 0x10000).toString(16).substring(1);
     }
     return s4() + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + s4() + s4();
   }
   
   function checkVariants(aValue) {
     if (aValue == '')
       aValue = '-';
 
     return aValue;
   }
   </script>

    $('.et_cc_wz_track').click(function(){
     if(et_cc_wz_pagename && et_cc_wz_area) {
       et_eC_Wrapper('y5EDSE','' + et_cc_wz_pagename, et_cc_wz_area);

   <script type="text/javascript">
    if(typeof et_cc_mode != 'undefined') {
     if(typeof etr_adding != 'undefined' && etr_adding == ''){
       etr_adding = '--'
     }
     sendCampaignControlEvent(et_cc_mode)
   }
 
   function sendCampaignControlEvent(aETCCMode) {
     
     if(typeof etr_variants == 'undefined') {
       etr_variants = '';
     }
     
     if(typeof etr_duration == 'undefined') {
       etr_duration = '--';
     }
     
     if(typeof etCommerce == 'undefined') {
       return;
     }
   
     if(aETCCMode == "prereceipt") {
       
       if(typeof et_basket_id == 'undefined') {
         return;
       }
   
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Insert To Basket auf Vorquittung */
       
       var product =
       {
         id      :etr_id,
         name    :etr_name,
         category:[etr_game,etr_gamename,etr_day],
         price   :etr_price,
         currency:'EUR',
         variants:
         {
           'Zusatzspiel' : checkVariants(etr_adding),
           'Laufzeit' : checkVariants(etr_duration),
           'Spezial' : checkVariants(etr_variants)
         }
       };
       etCommerce.sendEvent('insertToBasket', product, 1, et_basket_id);
       
       $('.et_cc_removeFromBasket').click(function(){
         /* Campaign Control Tracking: Remove From Basket auf Vorquittung */
         etCommerce.sendEvent('removeFromBasket', product, 1, et_basket_id);
       });
     
     } else if (aETCCMode == "receipt") {
       
       if(typeof et_basket_id == 'undefined') {
         return;
       }
     
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Order auf Quittung */
       
       var basket =
       {
         id: et_basket_id,
         products:[
         {
           product:
           {
             id      :etr_id,
             name    :etr_name,
             category:[etr_game,etr_gamename,etr_day],
             price   :etr_price,
             currency:'EUR',
             variants:
             {
               'Zusatzspiel' : checkVariants(etr_adding),
               'Laufzeit' : checkVariants(etr_duration),
               'Spezial' : checkVariants(etr_variants)
             }
           },
           quantity:1
         }]
       }
       
       var order =
       {
         orderNumber:getGlobalIdentifier(),
         status:'sale',
         orderPrice:etr_price,
         currency:'EUR',
         basket:basket,
         customerGroup:'Stammkunde',
         paymentMethod:etr_payment
       }
       etCommerce.sendEvent('order',order,'Warenkorb');
     
     } else if(aETCCMode == "register") {
       var guid = getGlobalIdentifier();
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Order auf Registrierung */
       console.log("register tracking");
       
       var basket =
       {
         id:guid,
         products:[
         {
           product:
           {
             id      :'REG',
             name    :'Registrierung',
             category:['Registrierung'],
             price   :'1.00',
             currency:'EUR',
             variants:{'Reg':'Reg'}
           },
           quantity:1
         }]
       };
   
       var order =
       {
         orderNumber:Date.now().toString(),
         status:'lead',
         orderPrice:'1.00',
         currency:'EUR',
         basket:basket,
         customerGroup:'18'
       };
       etCommerce.sendEvent('order',order,'Registrierung');
       
     }
   }
   
   /* Helper functions */
   
   function getGlobalIdentifier() {
     function s4() {
       return Math.floor((1 + Math.random()) * 0x10000).toString(16).substring(1);
     }
     return s4() + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + s4() + s4();
   }
   
   function checkVariants(aValue) {
     if (aValue == '')
       aValue = '-';
 
     return aValue;
   }

        <script type="text/javascript">
         var gConfigSpec_ = new de.multamedio.pfe.js.base.ConfigSpec(12,
       12, 'de');
 
     var gEurojackpotNormalTicketFeatures_ = {
       maxFieldCount: 10,
       ticketNo: {
         available: true
       },

         }

     'PFE.JS.TICKETS.LOGIC.GP_SET_FAILED_NO_GS_ACTIVE': 'Sie haben die Zusatzlotterie Gl&uuml;cksSpirale-Sieger-Chance aktiviert. Diese ist nur in Kombination mit der Gl&uuml;cksSpirale w&auml;hlbar. M&ouml;chten Sie beide Spielarten aktivieren?',

    $('.et_cc_wz_track').click(function(){
     if(et_cc_wz_pagename && et_cc_wz_area) {
       et_eC_Wrapper('y5EDSE','' + et_cc_wz_pagename, et_cc_wz_area);

   <script type="text/javascript">
    if(typeof et_cc_mode != 'undefined') {
     if(typeof etr_adding != 'undefined' && etr_adding == ''){
       etr_adding = '--'
     }
     sendCampaignControlEvent(et_cc_mode)
   }
 
   function sendCampaignControlEvent(aETCCMode) {
     
     if(typeof etr_variants == 'undefined') {
       etr_variants = '';
     }
     
     if(typeof etr_duration == 'undefined') {
       etr_duration = '--';
     }
     
     if(typeof etCommerce == 'undefined') {
       return;
     }
   
     if(aETCCMode == "prereceipt") {
       
       if(typeof et_basket_id == 'undefined') {
         return;
       }
   
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Insert To Basket auf Vorquittung */
       
       var product =
       {
         id      :etr_id,
         name    :etr_name,
         category:[etr_game,etr_gamename,etr_day],
         price   :etr_price,
         currency:'EUR',
         variants:
         {
           'Zusatzspiel' : checkVariants(etr_adding),
           'Laufzeit' : checkVariants(etr_duration),
           'Spezial' : checkVariants(etr_variants)
         }
       };
       etCommerce.sendEvent('insertToBasket', product, 1, et_basket_id);
       
       $('.et_cc_removeFromBasket').click(function(){
         /* Campaign Control Tracking: Remove From Basket auf Vorquittung */
         etCommerce.sendEvent('removeFromBasket', product, 1, et_basket_id);
       });
     
     } else if (aETCCMode == "receipt") {
       
       if(typeof et_basket_id == 'undefined') {
         return;
       }
     
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Order auf Quittung */
       
       var basket =
       {
         id: et_basket_id,
         products:[
         {
           product:
           {
             id      :etr_id,
             name    :etr_name,
             category:[etr_game,etr_gamename,etr_day],
             price   :etr_price,
             currency:'EUR',
             variants:
             {
               'Zusatzspiel' : checkVariants(etr_adding),
               'Laufzeit' : checkVariants(etr_duration),
               'Spezial' : checkVariants(etr_variants)
             }
           },
           quantity:1
         }]
       }
       
       var order =
       {
         orderNumber:getGlobalIdentifier(),
         status:'sale',
         orderPrice:etr_price,
         currency:'EUR',
         basket:basket,
         customerGroup:'Stammkunde',
         paymentMethod:etr_payment
       }
       etCommerce.sendEvent('order',order,'Warenkorb');
     
     } else if(aETCCMode == "register") {
       var guid = getGlobalIdentifier();
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Order auf Registrierung */
       console.log("register tracking");
       
       var basket =
       {
         id:guid,
         products:[
         {
           product:
           {
             id      :'REG',
             name    :'Registrierung',
             category:['Registrierung'],
             price   :'1.00',
             currency:'EUR',
             variants:{'Reg':'Reg'}
           },
           quantity:1
         }]
       };
   
       var order =
       {
         orderNumber:Date.now().toString(),
         status:'lead',
         orderPrice:'1.00',
         currency:'EUR',
         basket:basket,
         customerGroup:'18'
       };
       etCommerce.sendEvent('order',order,'Registrierung');
       
     }
   }
   
   /* Helper functions */
   
   function getGlobalIdentifier() {
     function s4() {
       return Math.floor((1 + Math.random()) * 0x10000).toString(16).substring(1);
     }
     return s4() + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + s4() + s4();
   }
   
   function checkVariants(aValue) {
     if (aValue == '')
       aValue = '-';
 
     return aValue;
   }

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $('.et_cc_wz_track').click(function(){
     if(et_cc_wz_pagename && et_cc_wz_area) {
       et_eC_Wrapper('y5EDSE','' + et_cc_wz_pagename, et_cc_wz_area);
       et_cc_wrapper('O74s6QuK7zIrJgBcSEB4se+sfIUGtSWS8xCIa9AmJVg=',{cc_pagename:'' + et_cc_wz_pagename})
     }
   });
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    if(typeof et_cc_mode != 'undefined') {
     if(typeof etr_adding != 'undefined' && etr_adding == ''){
       etr_adding = '--'
     }
     sendCampaignControlEvent(et_cc_mode)
   }
 
   function sendCampaignControlEvent(aETCCMode) {
     
     if(typeof etr_variants == 'undefined') {
       etr_variants = '';
     }
     
     if(typeof etr_duration == 'undefined') {
       etr_duration = '--';
     }
     
     if(typeof etCommerce == 'undefined') {
       return;
     }
   
     if(aETCCMode == "prereceipt") {
       
       if(typeof et_basket_id == 'undefined') {
         return;
       }
   
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Insert To Basket auf Vorquittung */
       
       var product =
       {
         id      :etr_id,
         name    :etr_name,
         category:[etr_game,etr_gamename,etr_day],
         price   :etr_price,
         currency:'EUR',
         variants:
         {
           'Zusatzspiel' : checkVariants(etr_adding),
           'Laufzeit' : checkVariants(etr_duration),
           'Spezial' : checkVariants(etr_variants)
         }
       };
       etCommerce.sendEvent('insertToBasket', product, 1, et_basket_id);
       
       $('.et_cc_removeFromBasket').click(function(){
         /* Campaign Control Tracking: Remove From Basket auf Vorquittung */
         etCommerce.sendEvent('removeFromBasket', product, 1, et_basket_id);
       });
     
     } else if (aETCCMode == "receipt") {
       
       if(typeof et_basket_id == 'undefined') {
         return;
       }
     
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Order auf Quittung */
       
       var basket =
       {
         id: et_basket_id,
         products:[
         {
           product:
           {
             id      :etr_id,
             name    :etr_name,
             category:[etr_game,etr_gamename,etr_day],
             price   :etr_price,
             currency:'EUR',
             variants:
             {
               'Zusatzspiel' : checkVariants(etr_adding),
               'Laufzeit' : checkVariants(etr_duration),
               'Spezial' : checkVariants(etr_variants)
             }
           },
           quantity:1
         }]
       }
       
       var order =
       {
         orderNumber:getGlobalIdentifier(),
         status:'sale',
         orderPrice:etr_price,
         currency:'EUR',
         basket:basket,
         customerGroup:'Stammkunde',
         paymentMethod:etr_payment
       }
       etCommerce.sendEvent('order',order,'Warenkorb');
     
     } else if(aETCCMode == "register") {
       var guid = getGlobalIdentifier();
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Order auf Registrierung */
       console.log("register tracking");
       
       var basket =
       {
         id:guid,
         products:[
         {
           product:
           {
             id      :'REG',
             name    :'Registrierung',
             category:['Registrierung'],
             price   :'1.00',
             currency:'EUR',
             variants:{'Reg':'Reg'}
           },
           quantity:1
         }]
       };
   
       var order =
       {
         orderNumber:Date.now().toString(),
         status:'lead',
         orderPrice:'1.00',
         currency:'EUR',
         basket:basket,
         customerGroup:'18'
       };
       etCommerce.sendEvent('order',order,'Registrierung');
       
     }
   }
   
   /* Helper functions */
   
   function getGlobalIdentifier() {
     function s4() {
       return Math.floor((1 + Math.random()) * 0x10000).toString(16).substring(1);
     }
     return s4() + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + s4() + s4();
   }
   
   function checkVariants(aValue) {
     if (aValue == '')
       aValue = '-';
 
     return aValue;
   }
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $('.et_cc_wz_track').click(function(){
     if(et_cc_wz_pagename && et_cc_wz_area) {
       et_eC_Wrapper('y5EDSE','' + et_cc_wz_pagename, et_cc_wz_area);
       et_cc_wrapper('O74s6QuK7zIrJgBcSEB4se+sfIUGtSWS8xCIa9AmJVg=',{cc_pagename:'' + et_cc_wz_pagename})
     }
   });
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    if(typeof et_cc_mode != 'undefined') {
     if(typeof etr_adding != 'undefined' && etr_adding == ''){
       etr_adding = '--'
     }
     sendCampaignControlEvent(et_cc_mode)
   }
 
   function sendCampaignControlEvent(aETCCMode) {
     
     if(typeof etr_variants == 'undefined') {
       etr_variants = '';
     }
     
     if(typeof etr_duration == 'undefined') {
       etr_duration = '--';
     }
     
     if(typeof etCommerce == 'undefined') {
       return;
     }
   
     if(aETCCMode == "prereceipt") {
       
       if(typeof et_basket_id == 'undefined') {
         return;
       }
   
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Insert To Basket auf Vorquittung */
       
       var product =
       {
         id      :etr_id,
         name    :etr_name,
         category:[etr_game,etr_gamename,etr_day],
         price   :etr_price,
         currency:'EUR',
         variants:
         {
           'Zusatzspiel' : checkVariants(etr_adding),
           'Laufzeit' : checkVariants(etr_duration),
           'Spezial' : checkVariants(etr_variants)
         }
       };
       etCommerce.sendEvent('insertToBasket', product, 1, et_basket_id);
       
       $('.et_cc_removeFromBasket').click(function(){
         /* Campaign Control Tracking: Remove From Basket auf Vorquittung */
         etCommerce.sendEvent('removeFromBasket', product, 1, et_basket_id);
       });
     
     } else if (aETCCMode == "receipt") {
       
       if(typeof et_basket_id == 'undefined') {
         return;
       }
     
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Order auf Quittung */
       
       var basket =
       {
         id: et_basket_id,
         products:[
         {
           product:
           {
             id      :etr_id,
             name    :etr_name,
             category:[etr_game,etr_gamename,etr_day],
             price   :etr_price,
             currency:'EUR',
             variants:
             {
               'Zusatzspiel' : checkVariants(etr_adding),
               'Laufzeit' : checkVariants(etr_duration),
               'Spezial' : checkVariants(etr_variants)
             }
           },
           quantity:1
         }]
       }
       
       var order =
       {
         orderNumber:getGlobalIdentifier(),
         status:'sale',
         orderPrice:etr_price,
         currency:'EUR',
         basket:basket,
         customerGroup:'Stammkunde',
         paymentMethod:etr_payment
       }
       etCommerce.sendEvent('order',order,'Warenkorb');
     
     } else if(aETCCMode == "register") {
       var guid = getGlobalIdentifier();
       /* Campaign Control Tracking: Order auf Registrierung */
       console.log("register tracking");
       
       var basket =
       {
         id:guid,
         products:[
         {
           product:
           {
             id      :'REG',
             name    :'Registrierung',
             category:['Registrierung'],
             price   :'1.00',
             currency:'EUR',
             variants:{'Reg':'Reg'}
           },
           quantity:1
         }]
       };
   
       var order =
       {
         orderNumber:Date.now().toString(),
         status:'lead',
         orderPrice:'1.00',
         currency:'EUR',
         basket:basket,
         customerGroup:'18'
       };
       etCommerce.sendEvent('order',order,'Registrierung');
       
     }
   }
   
   /* Helper functions */
   
   function getGlobalIdentifier() {
     function s4() {
       return Math.floor((1 + Math.random()) * 0x10000).toString(16).substring(1);
     }
     return s4() + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + s4() + s4();
   }
   
   function checkVariants(aValue) {
     if (aValue == '')
       aValue = '-';
 
     return aValue;
   }
   </script>
